Here is the situation:\\ \tt \\ \tt WHAT: Things at places\\ \tt LEFT: daisy\\ \tt RIGHT: lip gloss\\ \tt TOP: brightener\\ \tt BOTTOM: spoons\\ \tt CENTER: blouse\\ \tt NORTHWEST: melons\\ \tt NORTHEAST: pear\\ \tt SOUTHWEST: wrench\\ \tt SOUTHEAST: shovel\\ \tt HERE: jeans skirt\\ \tt THERE: cleanser\\ \tt NOWHERE: papaya\\ \tt EVERYWHERE: mascara\\ \tt INSIDE: mango\\ \tt OUTSIDE: post-it notes\\ \tt \\ \tt Questions from the questioner will start with QUESTIONER. Please reply in the form: ANSWER: <some text>\\ \tt \\ \tt I will also ask you questions. These questions will start with ME: . Please answer these questions with: ASIDE: <some text>\\ \tt \\ \tt Important: Give short, direct answers!\\ \tt \\ \tt Let us start. 
	  } 
	   } 
	   }
